 The 10 special days that changed Kejriwal's life from the foundation of his political career to his re-election as Chief Minister
 
 
 1
 April 5, 2011: Movement started with Anna On 5 April 2011, social activist Anna Hazare along with social activist Anna Hazare and other colleagues started a fast at Jantar Mantar to demand the Jan Lokpal Bill (civil Lokpal Bill)
 is anshan kaa prabhaav puure bharat main dikhaa tha or centre sarkaar bhi andolan ke aage aakhir main jhuki
 However, later the government did not stick to its promise and introduced a weak Lokpal
 yah andolan 12 dinon tak chalaa tha
 2
 2 oktober 2012: raajnneeti main aane kaa elaazarvind kejariwal ne apane raajnneetik safar kii aupchaarik shuruyaat 2 oktober 2012 ko kii thi
 He wore a Gandhi cap and inscribed on it, 'I am a common man'
 kejariwal ne isi din raajnneetik dal banane kii ghoshnaa kii or anna kii vichaardhaara se alag hokar sakriy raajnneeti kaa hissaa banane kii thaan lee
 3
 26 navambar 2012: aam aadmi party kaa gathservind kejariwal ne anna andolan se jude tamaam logon ke saath milakar aam aadmi party kaa gathan kiya
 Kejriwal's official announcement of its formation was on 26 November 2012 at Jantar Mantar, Delhi, on the occasion of the 63rd anniversary of the Indian Constitution Act
 4
 December 8, 2013: Politics of Chamki Kejriwal, Aam Aadmi Party convenor Arvind Kejriwal created history
 apane pehle hi chunaav main unki party ne dilli main 28 siten jeetkarrajnneetik panditon ke kayaason kogalat sabit kar diya
 Not only this, Kejriwal, who contested for the first time, defeated three-time Chief Minister Sheila Dikshit in Delhi by 22 thousand votes
 aam aadmi party kii is shandaar jeet ne nai raajnneeti kii shuruyaat maani jaati thi
 5
 28 disambar 2013: pehali baar CM bane kejarivaldilli ke mukhyamantri pad kii shapath lene ke saath hi 28 disambar 2013 kaa din kejariwal ke raajnneetik jivan kaa sabase ahm din he
 Kejriwal, who contested for the first time after reaching the Chief Minister's chair, announced to work as the voice of 'aam Aadmi' and took many big decisions during the 49-day rule
 6
 14 February 2014: Arvind Kejriwal resigned from his post on 14 February 2014, resigning from the post of Chief Minister, who held power for 49 days in the party
 congress ke samarthan se banaai gai sarkaar main sahyog na milane kaa hawala dete hue kejariwal ne pad se istipha diya
 According to the election promise, not getting the Jan Lokpal Bill passed in the Assembly was considered as the reason for this resignation
 haalanki loksabhaa chunaav bhi isaki vajah bane

 29 march 2014: road sho ke dauraan kejariwal ko padaa thappaservind kejariwal ko haryana main chunaav-prachaar ke dauraan ek shaks ne thappad maar diya

 8

 10 February 2015: Aam Aadmi Party's record-breaking victory: Aam Aadmi Party registered a historic victory in the assembly elections held in Delhi after the President's rule lasted for almost a year

 The United States has given the flight launch technology to India, which it itself is deploying in its aircraft ships, so that even larger fighter aircraft can fly from the ship itself
 isse bhartiya nausena ko takanic kii duniya main aage badhane main kaaphi madad milegi

 " america main republican party kii ore se raashtrapati pad ke pratyaashee donald trump kii 'america first' par aadhaarit videsh niti se jude bayanon ke maddenzar bharat tathaa anya asian deshon main atakalon kaa bazaar garm he ki trump ke jeetne kii sthiti main asia main america kii upasthiti kam kii ja sakati he
 Trump has said that Japan and South Korea, the allies of the US, should spend more money to protect themselves
 unhone march maheene main 'neuyark times' ko die ek saakshaatkaar main kaha tha ki vah japan main bane beson se america fouj ko waapas bula sakate hai, or unhone is vichaar ko bhi hawa di thi ki vah japan or dakshin korea ko khud kaa parmaanu shastraagaar viksit karne de sakate hai
 Manoj Ladwa, a London-based political strategist who served as Director of Communications during Prime Minister Narendra Modi's election campaign, says Trump has sent contradictory messages to India
 unhone bataaya, "ek taraf trump kaa kahana he ki vah bharat ke saath vyapaarik sambandhon ko mahatv dete hai, lekin saath hi bhartiya kol centre main kaam karne waalon kaa mazaaq bhi udaate hai, or us pratiyogi maahaul kii andekhi karte hai, jo bharat ke saath sahyog karne par america ko hasil ho saktaa he
 
 
 Therefore, his views are not clear in a world where strong and mature diplomacy is needed
 
 
 " By the way, in the case of military cooperation, the help of the US is most important for India, which the US is giving to make it its largest aircraft carrier
